Status Duration Determination
C2/8B7D: 64 0F        STZ $0F
C2/8B7F: A5 58        LDA $58
C2/8B81: 29 7F        AND #$7F
C2/8B83: 0A           ASL             
C2/8B84: 26 0F        ROL $0F
C2/8B86: 85 0E        STA $0E         $0E = (bits 0-6 of $58) * 2 
C2/8B88: AD E5 7B     LDA $7BE5
C2/8B8B: 20 C0 01     JSR $01C0       (Attacker Level / 4)
C2/8B8E: 18           CLC 
C2/8B8F: 65 0E        ADC $0E
C2/8B91: 85 0E        STA $0E         $0E + (Attacker Level / 4)
C2/8B93: A5 0F        LDA $0F
C2/8B95: 69 00        ADC #$00
C2/8B97: F0 04        BEQ $8B9D
C2/8B99: A9 FF        LDA #$FF
C2/8B9B: 85 0E        STA $0E         (Max $0E = 255)
C2/8B9D: A5 58        LDA $58
C2/8B9F: 30 28        BMI $8BC9       (If $58 >= 80h, ignore target effects)
C2/8BA1: A6 49        LDX $49
C2/8BA3: BD 65 20     LDA $2065,X
C2/8BA6: 29 20        AND #$20        (Target Creature Type = Heavy?)
C2/8BA8: F0 06        BEQ $8BB0 
C2/8BAA: A9 1E        LDA #$1E
C2/8BAC: 85 0E        STA $0E         (If target is Heavy, $0E = 1Eh)
C2/8BAE: 80 19        BRA $8BC9
C2/8BB0: 18           CLC 
C2/8BB1: BD 02 20     LDA $2002,X
C2/8BB4: 7D 78 20     ADC $2078,X
C2/8BB7: 20 C0 01     JSR $01C0       (Target Level / 4)
C2/8BBA: 85 0F        STA $0F
C2/8BBC: 38           SEC 
C2/8BBD: A5 0E        LDA $0E
C2/8BBF: E5 0F        SBC $0F         ($58 * 2 + (Attacker Level / 4) - (Target Level / 4))
C2/8BC1: F0 02        BEQ $8BC5
C2/8BC3: B0 02        BCS $8BC7
C2/8BC5: A9 01        LDA #$01        (Minimum $0E = 1)
C2/8BC7: 85 0E        STA $0E
C2/8BC9: A5 0E        LDA $0E
C2/8BCB: 8D D8 3E     STA $3ED8
C2/8BCE: 60           RTS
